         <div class="home-block get-help block block-block-content block-block-content31fcc259-6397-4136-a5ba-829798c62dd2" id="block-homeblockgethelp">
          <h2 class="visually-hidden">
           Home block - Get Help
          </h2>
          <div class="block-content">
           <div class="samhsa-block-title field field--name-field-title field--type-string field--label-hidden field__item">
            <h2>
             Get Help
            </h2>
           </div>
           <div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-body field--type-text-with-summary field--label-hidden field__item">
            <ul class="get-help-list">
             <li>
              <h3>
               <a class="fix-height" href="https://findtreatment.gov/">
                FindTreatment.gov
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p>
               Millions of Americans have a substance use disorder.
              </p>
              <p class="helpline-phone">
               <a href="https://findtreatment.gov/">
                Find a facility near you
               </a>
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <h3>
               <a class="fix-height" href="https://suicidepreventionlifeline.org/">
                National Suicide Prevention Lifeline
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p>
               Free and confidential support for people in distress, 24/7.
              </p>
              <p class="helpline-phone">
               <a href="tel:18002738255">
                1-800-273-TALK (8255)
               </a>
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <h3>
               <a class="fix-height" href="https://findtreatment.samhsa.gov/">
                Behavioral Health Treatment Service Locator
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p>
               Find treatment facilities confidentially, 24/7.
              </p>
              <p class="helpline-phone">
               <a href="https://findtreatment.samhsa.gov/">
                Find a location near you
               </a>
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <h3>
               <a class="fix-height" href="https://www.samhsa.gov/find-help/national-helpline">
                National Helpline
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p>
               Treatment referral and information, 24/7.
              </p>
              <p class="helpline-phone">
               <a href="tel:18006624357" id="anch_65">
                1-800-662-HELP (4357)
               </a>
              </p>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>

         <div class="home-block block block-block-content block-block-contenta71cd1f7-3d23-4c29-8742-f764f66b69c4" id="block-officesandcentershomepageblock">
          <h2 class="visually-hidden">
           Offices and Centers - Homepage block
          </h2>
          <div class="block-content">
           <div class="samhsa-block-title field field--name-field-title field--type-string field--label-hidden field__item">
            <h2>
             Our Offices and Centers
            </h2>
           </div>
           <div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-body field--type-text-with-summary field--label-hidden field__item">
            <ul class="centers-offices-items">
             <li class="centers-offices-item">
              <h3 class="centers-offices-item-title">
               <a href="//www.samhsa.gov/about-us/who-we-are/offices-centers/oas">
                Office of the Assistant Secretary (OAS)
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p>
               OAS reports to the Secretary of the Department of Health and Human Services and is responsible for managing and directing SAMHSA.
              </p>
             </li>
             <li class="centers-offices-item">
              <h3 class="centers-offices-item-title">
               <a href="//www.samhsa.gov/about-us/who-we-are/offices-centers/nmhsupl">
                National Mental Health Substance Use and Policy Laboratory (NMHSUPL)
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p>
               Promotes evidence-based practices and service delivery models.
              </p>
             </li>
             <li class="centers-offices-item">
              <h3 class="centers-offices-item-title">
               <a href="//www.samhsa.gov/about-us/who-we-are/offices-centers/ofr">
                Office of Financial Resources (OFR)
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p>
               OFR develops and implements the policies and programs of the Assistant Secretary.
              </p>
             </li>
             <li class="centers-offices-item">
              <h3 class="centers-offices-item-title">
               <a href="//www.samhsa.gov/about-us/who-we-are/offices-centers/omto">
                Office of Management, Technology, and Operations (OMTO)
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p>
               OMTO oversees and supports SAMHSA needs.
              </p>
             </li>
             <li class="centers-offices-item">
              <h3 class="centers-offices-item-title">
               <a href="//www.samhsa.gov/about-us/who-we-are/offices-centers/oc">
                Office of Communications (OC)
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p>
               OC is SAMHSA's voice and face to the public.
              </p>
             </li>
            </ul>
            <ul class="centers-offices-items">
             <li class="centers-offices-item">
              <h3 class="centers-offices-item-title">
               <a href="//www.samhsa.gov/about-us/who-we-are/offices-centers/cmhs">
                Center for Mental Health Services (CMHS)
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p>
               CMHS leads federal efforts to promote the prevention and treatment of mental disorders.
              </p>
             </li>
             <li class="centers-offices-item">
              <h3 class="centers-offices-item-title">
               <a href="//www.samhsa.gov/about-us/who-we-are/offices-centers/csap">
                Center for Substance Abuse Prevention (CSAP)
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p>
               The mission of CSAP is to improve behavioral health through evidence-based prevention approaches.
              </p>
             </li>
             <li class="centers-offices-item">
              <h3 class="centers-offices-item-title">
               <a href="//www.samhsa.gov/about-us/who-we-are/offices-centers/csat">
                Center for Substance Abuse Treatment (CSAT)
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p>
               CSAT promotes community-based substance abuse treatment and recovery services for individuals and families in every community.
              </p>
             </li>
             <li class="centers-offices-item">
              <h3 class="centers-offices-item-title">
               <a href="//www.samhsa.gov/about-us/who-we-are/offices-centers/cbhsq">
                Center for Behavioral Health Statistics and Quality (CBHSQ)
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p>
               CBHSQ is the government’s lead agency for behavioral health statistics, as designated by the Office of Management and Budget.
              </p>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
